Regression Test for Non-Legacy Mail Decryption Failure\n\n## Overview\nThis regression test demonstrates a critical bug in the tutanota mail client where non-legacy mails with owner-encrypted session keys fail to decrypt their related entities when loaded in batch mode.\n\n## Bug Description\n**Issue:** Non-legacy mails fail to decrypt their content (body, recipients, attachments) when loaded via batch operations.\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Opening non-legacy mails in inbox shows blank message bodies\n- Reply-to addresses and recipient lists are missing\n- Mail indexer/search encounters \"Missing (batch mode)\n2. Session keys from each mail's `_ownerEncSessionKey` are NOT extracted\n3. `loadInChunks()` calls `loadMultiple()` without the session keys map\n4. `EntityRestClient._decryptMapAndMigrate()` cannot decrypt entities\n5. `SessionKeyNotFoundError` is thrown and caught silently\n6. Result: Decrypted entities have `_errors` set on encrypted fields\n7. Users see blank/missing mail content\n\n## Test Structure\n\nThe regression test (`/workspace/regression_test.test.ts`) is a self-contained Jest test with three test cases:\n\n### Test 1: Demonstrate the Bug\n- Shows the code flow where session keys are NOT propagated\n- Verifies that the bug exists in batch loading mode\n- Uses comments to document the expected vs. actual behavior\n\n### Test 2: Document the Correct Pattern\n- Explains how single-load correctly propagates session keys\n- Shows the proper use of `providedOwnerEncSessionKeys` parameter\n- Demonstrates the contrast with batch loading\n\n### Test 3: Identify Exact Location and Impact\n- Pinpoints the exact bug location in the source code\n- Documents all three mail loading paths (legacy, blob, draft)\n- Explains why only batch loading is affected\n- Describes the user-facing impact\n\n## How to Run the Test\n\n```bash\nnpx jest --timeout=60000 /workspace/regression_test.test.ts\n```\n\nExpected output:\n```\nPASS ./regression_test.test.ts\n  Regression: Non-legacy mail batch loading session key propagation\n    ✓ should demonstrate that loadMailDetails does not propagate session keys to batch loading\n    ✓ should document the correct single-load pattern that works\n    ✓ should identify the exact bug location and impact\n\nTest Suites: 1 passed, 1 total\nTests:       3 passed, 3 total\n```\n\n## Fix Strategy\n\nTo fix this bug:\n\n1. **Modify `loadMailDetails()` (lines 726-756)**\n   - Extract session keys from mails into a Map during iteration\n   - Pass session keys to `loadInChunks()` for each mail type (blob/draft)\n\n2. **Modify `loadInChunks()` (lines 780-790)**\n   - Accept `providedOwnerEncSessionKeys` as optional parameter\n   -
